namespace = migration_fixes

migration_fixes.1 = {
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {

			}
			set_variable = migration_fixes_active

			limit = {
				OR = {

			if = {
				limit = {
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:welsh
				}
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = ROOT
						is_capital = no
						OR = {
							is_incorporated = yes
							NOT = { has_state_trait = state_trait_severe_malaria }
							owner = { has_technology_researched = quinine }
						}
						OR = {
							is_incorporated = yes
							is_split_state = no
							owner = { NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_no_colonial_affairs } }
							NOT = { any_neighbouring_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } }
						}
						OR = {
							is_isolated_from_market = no
							AND = {
								is_coastal = yes
								has_building = building_port
							}
						}
						NOT = { any_scope_pop = { culture = cu:welsh } }
					}
					save_temporary_scope_as = migration_fixes_welsh_state
					scope:migration_fixes_capital = {
						random_scope_pop = {
							limit = {
								culture = cu:welsh
								NOT = { is_pop_type = slaves }
							}
							move_pop = scope:migration_fixes_welsh_state

						owner = ROOT
						is_capital = no
						OR = {
							is_incorporated = yes
							NOT = { has_state_trait = state_trait_severe_malaria }
							owner = { has_technology_researched = quinine }
						}
						OR = {
							is_incorporated = yes
							is_split_state = no
							owner = { NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_no_colonial_affairs } }
							NOT = { any_neighbouring_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } }
						}
						OR = {
							is_isolated_from_market = no
							AND = {
								is_coastal = yes
								has_building = building_port
							}
						}
						NOT = { any_scope_pop = { culture = cu:kirgiz } }
					}
					save_temporary_scope_as = migration_fixes_kirgiz_state
					scope:migration_fixes_capital = {
						random_scope_pop = {
							limit = {
								culture = cu:kirgiz
								NOT = { is_pop_type = slaves }
							}
							move_pop = scope:migration_fixes_kirgiz_state
						}

									culture = cu:marathi
								}
								move_pop = scope:migration_fixes_capital
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:pathan
				}
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = ROOT
						is_capital = no
						OR = {
							is_incorporated = yes
							NOT = { has_state_trait = state_trait_severe_malaria }
							owner = { has_technology_researched = quinine }
						}
						OR = {
							is_incorporated = yes
							is_split_state = no
							owner = { NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_no_colonial_affairs } }
							NOT = { any_neighbouring_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } }
						}
						OR = {
							is_isolated_from_market = no
							AND = {
								is_coastal = yes
								has_building = building_port
							}
						}
						NOT = { any_scope_pop = { culture = cu:pathan } }
					}
					save_temporary_scope_as = migration_fixes_pathan_state
					scope:migration_fixes_capital = {
						random_scope_pop = {
							limit = {
								culture = cu:pathan
								NOT = { is_pop_type = slaves }
							}
							move_pop = scope:migration_fixes_pathan_state
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_incorporated = no
						}
						scope:migration_fixes_pathan_state = {
							every_scope_pop = {
								limit = {
									culture = cu:pathan
								}
								move_pop = scope:migration_fixes_capital
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = migration_fixes.1
			days = 1
		}
	}
}
